The carpet in the corridor is dirty, and the spider webs in the room have not been swept for a long time. The stains on the doors and windows are never wiped. The bathroom door handle is sticky to the touch... I can't complain... None of the sockets in the room are correct, and one of the table lamps is broken... There is no exhaust in the whole room. After going to the toilet, you can only open the door and window for ventilation. The windows in the corridor are basically locked. There is no exhaust in the whole hotel. After breakfast in the morning, I went back to the room and there were all kinds of stinky smells all the way! ! I don't know if the owner used to run a homestay? It's really not appropriate to use the standards of a homestay to do such a large resort hotel! I will never go there again! !

Let me complain about the breakfast again. There are very few varieties and the quality is very poor. You can eat enough, but there is really nothing to eat... The day with the most people on holidays is just like fleeing from war, very terrible! It can be seen that this hotel has no reception capacity at all... They even pushed a trash can next to collect the plates, speechless.

The facilities in the hotel park are also in a dilapidated state. We didn't go on the so-called free two-hour ride. There is really nothing to see. The ****s are overgrown and the facilities have been abandoned for many years. As I said, things can be old, but they cannot be maintained.

To be honest, the service attitude of the hotel waiters is very good, but they just can't solve the problem. This can't be used as an excuse for the epidemic. How long has the epidemic been over?
